msg:I went to the new Internet celebrity hotel in Nanjing during the weekend. The overall evaluation is that the facilities and equipment of the so-called 7-star hotel are really good, but the service level is below 3 stars.
Let me talk about a few details:
1) About booking: To arrange a 3-day and 2-night itinerary, it is actually necessary to book through 2 different online channels. During the booking process, I made countless phone calls. The hotel reservation depar**ent pushed through third-party channels.
2) The hotel is basically in the mountains, and the transportation is definitely inconvenient, unless it is more convenient to drive by yourself. The breakfast buffet in the morning is good, but because there are many teams eating breakfast together, the dining experience of individual tourists must be poor. It is recommended to eat after 9:00 to avoid the team. The evening buffet is really not recommended. Although there is a discounted price of 128 yuan per person for guests, there are still too many people, the dining experience is poor, the dishes are poor, and the price/performance ratio is even worse. If you must eat in the hotel, go to the a la carte restaurant, of course the price will be higher.
3) The hotel reception is the most ridiculous service. After collecting the deposit, I did not give a deposit slip. I asked, and replied that you would lose it if you left it, or it would be safe to leave it at the front desk. So what is the front desk reception process like? How did you come up with such a ridiculous reason? What do you have that customers trust? My final conclusion is that it is not trustworthy at all. Because I arranged for my parents to move in the next day, the old man is relatively old, and I am afraid of trouble. I obviously went through all the procedures in advance and paid the deposit, but when the old man moved in, he was still talking about it. He called me one by one to confirm , Is there a handover between the front desk staff of the hotel? What is the position of customer feedback and demands?
4) The hot spring was one of the reasons I chose to stay at that time, but the site is actually 3 small indoor pools (red wine pool/lavender pool/and swimming pool and children's play pool), and the bigger baths are just. Proofing at 22 o'clock in the evening, you are not allowed to enter after 21:30. I went there after about 20:30 one day. I went to take a bath after soaking in the hot spring. When I came out, the swimsuit on the stool of the locker had been collected by the waiter who was in a hurry to get off work. It's funny how you can rush to pack things up even though the customer hasn't left yet.
Many inexplicable details will not be detailed one by one. Generally speaking, there are many hotels with good hardware and special services. There is no need to come to a hotel with such a service level and inconvenient transportation. It is not recommended.
